### <a id="inductive-types-h-s-p-and-v">Inductive Types H, S, P, and V</a>

This section presents the [UALib.Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`).

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

<!-- If C₁ and C₂ are closure operators on classes of structures, let us say that C₁ ≤ C₂ if for every class 𝒦 we have C₁(𝒦) ⊆ C₂(𝒦). -->

A **variety** is a class 𝒦 of algebras in a fixed signature that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images (H), subalgebras (S), and arbitrary products (P).  That is, 𝒦 is a variety if and only if `H S P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`.

This module defines what we have found to be the most useful inductive types representing the closure operators H, S, and P. Separately, we define the inductive type `V` for simultaneously representing closure under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

<!-- ; consequently, we expect `V 𝒦 ≡ H (S (P 𝒦))` to hold for each class 𝒦 of algebras of a fixed signature. classes of algebras that are closed under H, S, P, and V ≡ HSP. -->

#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphism closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2755" class="Comment">--Closure wrt H</a>

  <a id="H.hiso"></a><a id="3073" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3073" class="InductiveConstructor">hiso</a>  <a id="3079" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3081" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3082" <!-- We say that a class 𝒦 is **closed under** `H` (or `H`-**closed**) provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

--------------------------------

#### <a id="subalgebra-closure">Subalgebra closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras that are closed under the taking of subalgebras as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3521" class="Comment">--Closure wrt S</a>
<a id="3537" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="3542" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3544" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3545" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3547" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3547" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3549" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3551" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="3559" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="3561" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3561" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3563" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3565" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3570" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3571" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3579" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3581" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3582" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3584" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3585" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="3588" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3589" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3592" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="3595" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3600" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3601" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3612" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3614" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3547" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3615" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3617" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3618" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3620" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3621" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="3624" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3625" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3627" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3547" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3630" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3633" class="Keyword">where</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3561" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `S` (or `S`-**closed**) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` -->

-----------------------------------------

#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras closed under arbitrary products is the following. 

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4325" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="4330" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4332" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4333" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4335" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4337" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4339" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="4347" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4349" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4350" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4352" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4354" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4359" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4360" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4368" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4370" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4371" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4373" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4374" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="4377" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4378" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4381" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="4384" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4389" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4390" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4398" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4399" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4401" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4403" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4404" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4406" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4407" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4409" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4410" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="4413" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4414" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4416" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4418" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4419" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4422" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="P.pbase"></a><a id="4430" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4430" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a>  <a id="4437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4439" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4440" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4442" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4444" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4452" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4454" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4455" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4457" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4459" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4461" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4463" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4465" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4467" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="4476" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4478" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4480" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4482" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4484" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="P.prodw"></a><a id="4715" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4715" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a>  <a id="4722" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4724" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4725" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4779" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4781" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4782" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4784" class="Symbol">→</a> <a class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4864" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4825" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4866" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4868" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4825" </pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `P` (or `P`-**closed**) provided `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

-----------------------------------------------

#### <a id="variety-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will typically denote it by `V`.

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="5605" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="5610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5610" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5612" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5613" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5615" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5617" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5619" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5627" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5629" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5631" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5633" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5639" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5647" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5649" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5650" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5652" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5653" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="5656" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5657" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5660" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="5663" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5668" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5669" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5677" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5678" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5680" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5682" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5683" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5685" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5686" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5688" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="5691" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5692" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5694" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5696" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5697" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5700" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="V.vbase"></a><a id="5708" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5708" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a>  <a id="5715" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5717" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5718" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5718" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5720" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5722" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5730" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5732" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5733" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5735" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5737" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5718" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5739" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5741" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5629" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5743" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5745" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="5754" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5718" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5756" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5758" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5760" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5610" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5762" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5629" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

-------------------------------

#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties since we will need them later.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6701" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s expansive.</a>
<a id="P-expa"></a><a id="6760" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6760" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="6767" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6769" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6770" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6770" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6772" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6774" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6782" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6784" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6784" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6786" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6788" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6793" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6794" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6802" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6770" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6804" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6805" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6807" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="6810" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6770" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6811" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="6815" class="Symbol">→</a>       <a id="6823" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6784" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6825" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6827" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="6828" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6829" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6770" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6830" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6832" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6770" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6833" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6835" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6784" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="6838" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6760" class="Function">P-expa</a><a id="6844" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6845" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6845" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6846" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6848" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6848" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="6849" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6851" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6852" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6852" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6853" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6855" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6855" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="6858" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6860" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4798" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="6865" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6866" class="Argument">𝑨</a> <a id="6868" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6870" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6871" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6880" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6852" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6882" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6845" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6883" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="6886" class="Argument">𝑩</a> <a id="6888" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6890" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6852" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6891" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6893" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6894" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4430" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="6900" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6855" class="Bound">KA</a><a id="6902" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6904" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6905" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="6911" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="6921" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6924" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s idempotent.</a>

<a id="7485" class="Comment">-- S is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s monotone.</a>

<a id="7885" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7892" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7892" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7898" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3906" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7903" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7903" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7905" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7905" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7907" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7909" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7911" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3906" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7916" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7917" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7924" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7892" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7929" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7903" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7930" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7932" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7905" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="subalgebra→S"></a><a id="8144" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8144" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="8157" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8159" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8160" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8160" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8162" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8162" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8164" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8166" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="8174" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8176" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8176" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8178" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8180" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8185" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8186" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8194" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8160" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8196" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8197" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8199" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="8202" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8160" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8203" class="Symbol">)}</a>
               <a id="8221" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8222" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8222" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8224" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8226" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8234" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8235" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8160" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8237" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="8239" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8162" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8240" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8242" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8243" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8245" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8247" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8222" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8249" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2536" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="8269" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8176" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
             <a id="8284" class="Comment">----------------------------------------------------------</a>

  <a id="9901" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="9910" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9910" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="9913" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9915" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9884" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9917" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2536" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="9937" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8631" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

   <a id="10011" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10011" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10016" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10018" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9884" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10020" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="10022" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10024" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9966" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10027" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="10032" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10011" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10037" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10039" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10043" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10045" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10049" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9910" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10052" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

The next lemma would be too obvoius to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="12961" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12961" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12966" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12968" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12651" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12971" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="12973" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12591" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
  <a id="12977" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12961" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12982" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12984" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3811" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="12992" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12651" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12995" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12591" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="12997" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12998" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="13004" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="13014" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13016" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12606" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the short term objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

<pre class="Agda">

    <a id="14087" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14060" class="Function">i</a> <a id="14089" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14091" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="14093" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14093" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14095" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14095" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14097" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14099" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14100" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13948" class="Function">h</a> <a id="14102" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14095" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14103" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14105" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14106" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14093" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14108" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14095" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14109" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="14139" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14115" class="Function">ii</a> <a id="14142" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14144" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#9558" class="Function">embedding-lift</a><a id="14158" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14159" class="Argument">𝓠</a> <a id="14161" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14163" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13474" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14171" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14173" class="Argument">𝓘</a> <a id="14175" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14177" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13477"     <a id="14226" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14226" class="Function">iii</a> <a id="14230" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14232" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Basic.html#2093" class="Function">is-homomorphism</a> <a id="14248" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14249" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14251" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13635" class="Function">SA</a><a id="14253" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14255" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14256" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14258" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13590" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="14259" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14261" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14060" class="Function">i</a>
    <a id="14267" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14226" class="Function">iii</a> <a id="14271" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14273" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="14275" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14275" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="14277" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14277" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="14279" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14281" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2277" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="14285" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="14287" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14287" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14289" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14291" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14292" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="14296" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="14298" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13871" class="Function">SA≤𝒜</a> <a id="14303" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14287" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14305" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a><a id="14306" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14308" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14275" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="14310" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="14313" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14313" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14315" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14317" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14277" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="14319" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14313" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14321" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14287" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14322" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14326" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14326" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="14328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14330" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14332" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13491" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14334" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="14336" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14338" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13635" class="Function">SA</a>
  <a id="14343" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14326" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="14345" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14347" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6161" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="14350" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2277" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="14354" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13743" class="Function">B≅SA</a>

</pre>

#### PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this module with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play in our formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="SP⊆V"></a><a id="17802" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17802" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17807" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17809" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17810" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17810" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17812" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17812" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="17814" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17816" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="17824" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17826" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17826" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17828" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17830" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17835" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17836" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17844" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17810" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17846" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17847" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17849" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="17852" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17810" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17853" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="17857" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="17862" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="17863" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17864" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17810" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17866" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="17868" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17812" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17869" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17871" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17810" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17873" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="17875" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17812" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17876" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17878" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17879" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="17880" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17881" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17810" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17882" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17884" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17812" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17885" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17887" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17826" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17888" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17890" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="17892" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5610" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="17893" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17894" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17810" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17895" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17897" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17812" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17898" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17900" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17826" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
<a id="17902" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17802" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17907" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17908" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3641" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="17913" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17914" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17914" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17915" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17917" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17917" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="17922" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17924" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17926" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17458" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="17930" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17931" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4878" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="17937" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17917" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="17943" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="17953" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="17955" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17802" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17960" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17961" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3698" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="17966" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17967" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17967" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17968" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17970" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17970" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17971" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17973" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17975" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5832" class="InductiveConstructor">vliftw</a> <a id="17982" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17983" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17802" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17988" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17970" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17989" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="products-of-classes">Products of classes</a>

Above we proved PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦).  It is slightly more painful to prove that the product of *all* algebras in the class S(𝒦) is a member of SP(𝒦). That is,

```agda
⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)
```

This is mainly due to the fact that it's not obvious (at least not to this author-coder) what should be the type of the product of all members of a class of algebras.  After a few false starts, eventually the right type revealed itself.  Of course, now that we have it in our hands, it seems rather obvious.

We now describe the this type of product of all algebras in an arbitrary class 𝒦 of algebras of the same signature.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="18843" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product"></a><a id="18850" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18850" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="18864" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18865" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18865" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18867" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18869" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18877" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18879" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18879" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18881" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18883" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18888" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18889" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18897" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18865" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18899" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18900" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18902" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18903" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="18906" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18865" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18907" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18910" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="18918" class="Comment">-- ℑ serves as the index of the product</a>
 <a id="class-product.ℑ"></a><a id="18959" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18959" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18961" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18963" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18964" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18964" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18966" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18968" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18976" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18978" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="18981" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18986" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18987" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18995" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18964" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18997" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18998" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19000" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19003" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18964" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19004" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19006" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19008" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19009" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19012" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18964" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19013" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19015" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
 <a id="19018" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18959" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19020" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19021" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19021" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19022" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19024" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19024" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19026" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19028" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="19030" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19030" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19032" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="19034" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19035" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19043" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19021" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19045" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19046" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19048" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="19050" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19030" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19052" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19054" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19024" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="19059" class="Comment">-- 𝔄 produces an algebra for each index (i : ℑ).</a>
 <a id="class-product.𝔄"></a><a id="19109" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19109" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19111" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19113" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19114" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19114" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19116" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19118" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19126" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19128" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19128" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19130" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19132" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19137" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19138" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19146" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19114" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19148" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19149" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19151" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19154" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19114" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19155" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19158" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19160" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18959" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19162" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19128" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19164" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19166" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19174" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19114" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19176" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="19179" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19109" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="19180" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19181" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19181" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19182" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19184" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19184" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19185" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19187" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19189" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="19191" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19192" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19192" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19194" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19196" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19197" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18959" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19199" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19184" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19200" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19203" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19205" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="19207" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19192" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19209" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

 <a id="19213" class="Comment">-- The product of all members of 𝒦 can be written simply as follows:</a>
 <a id="class-product.class-product"></a><a id="19283" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19283" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="19297" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19299" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19300" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19300" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19302" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19304" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19312" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19314" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19316" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19321" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19322" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19330" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19300" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19332" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19333" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19335" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19338" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19300" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19339" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19341" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19343" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19351" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19352" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19355" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19300" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19356" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19358" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="19361" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19283" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="19375" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19376" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19376" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19377" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19379" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19379" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19381" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19383" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="19385" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19387" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19109" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="19388" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19389" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19376" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19390" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19392" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19379" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19393" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19395" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="19399" class="Comment">-- ...or, more explicitly, here is the expansion of this indexed product.</a>
 <a id="class-product.class-product&#39;"></a><a id="19474" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19474" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="19489" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19491" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19492" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19492" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19494" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19496" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19504" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19506" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19508" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19513" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19514" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19522" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19492" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19524" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19525" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19527" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19530" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19492" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19531" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19533" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19535" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19543" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19544" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19547" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19492" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19548" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19550" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="19553" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19474" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a><a id="19567" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19568" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19568" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19569" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19571" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19571" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19573" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19575" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="19577" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="19579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19580" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19580" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19582" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19584" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19585" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="19587" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19587" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19589" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="19591" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19592" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19600" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19568" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19602" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19603" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19605" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="19607" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19587" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19609" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19611" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19571" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19612" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19615" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19617" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="19619" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19580" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19621" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Notice that, if `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, then we can think of the pair `(𝑨 , p) ∈ ℑ 𝒦` as an index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p)` (which is obviously `𝑨`) as the projection of the product `⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} )` onto the `(𝑨 , p)`-th component.

#### ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)
Finally, we prove the result that plays a leading role in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem---namely, that our newly defined class product ⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} ) belongs to SP(𝒦).

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="20093" class="Comment">-- The product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
<a id="20158" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product-inclusions"></a><a id="20165" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20165" class="Module">class-product-inclusions</a> <a id="20190" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20191" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="20193" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20195" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="20203" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20205" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20206" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20206" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="20208" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20210" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="20215" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20216" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20224" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="20226" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="20227" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20229" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="20232" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20233" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="20236" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="20244" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20249" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18850" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="20263" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20264" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="20266" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20268" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20269" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20271" class="Argument">𝒦</a> <a id="20273" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20275" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20206" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20276" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="20429" class="Keyword">where</a>

   <a id="21037" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#21037" class="Function">⨅llA≅cpK</a> <a id="21046" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21048" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="21050" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20534" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21054" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="21056" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19283" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="21070" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21071" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="21072" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21073" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21074" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21076" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21077" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21079" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20206" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21080" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="21085" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#21037" class="Function">⨅llA≅cpK</a> <a id="21094" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21096" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6161" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="21099" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2277" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="21103" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20926" class="Function">llA≅A</a>

 <a id="21111" class="Comment">-- So, since PS⊆SP, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>

  <a id="21255" class="Symbol">→</a>                  <a id="21274" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19283" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="21288" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21289" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="21290" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21291" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21292" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21294" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21295" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21297" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20206" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21298" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21300" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="21302" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21303" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="21304" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21305" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="21308" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21309" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21311" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="21314" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21315" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21317" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21318" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="21319" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21320" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21321" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21323" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="21326" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20191" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21327" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21329" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20206" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21330" class="Symbol">))</a>
